  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Mucize Lezzetler is now on your TVs! 🚀 

Appcent and <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/company/arcelikturkiye?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Arçelik Türkiye</a> partnered to bring delicious recipes and rich culinary content to Google TV!
 
Why Google TV? 
• To create a fresh platform for a beloved cooking project.
• To leverage Arçelik's strong presence in the Google TV market with an innovative step.

This collaboration transformed the remote control into more than just a tool—it’s now a personal guide, delivering intuitive navigation and a seamless, delightful experience. This is the result of innovation fueled by shared passion.

We’d like to extend a special thank you to <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/selcuk-avci?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Selçuk Avcı</a>, <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/boradenizci?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Bora Denizci</a>, <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/dilara-morhayim-k%C3%B6semen-23969852?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Dilara Morhayim Kösemen</a>, and Edanur Sandalcı Kantar from Arçelik for their invaluable contributions and trust in choosing us to bring this vision to life.

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fappcent&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Appcent</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2FarAexelik&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Arçelik</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fgoogletv&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#GoogleTV</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fmucizelezzetler&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#MucizeLezzetler</a></p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">How can small businesses launch and promote loyalty programs effectively? 🤔

Launching a <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Floyalty&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#loyalty</a> program doesn’t have to be complicated! Here are some key steps small businesses can take to ensure success:

🟦 Make sure your loyalty program is easy to understand and join. Customers should be able to participate without hassle
🟦 Let your customers know about the benefits of joining. Use emails, social media, and in-store promotions to spread the word.
🟦 Tailor rewards based on your customers' preferences to make them feel valued and special. This will increase engagement and loyalty.
🟦 Keep your customers excited about the program by regularly updating offers and communicating with them. 

Reach out to Appcent to launch your loyalty program today!

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Did you know how global brands implement their loyalty programs? Here’s an inspiring example: <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fstarbucks&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Starbucks</a> 🧋

When you think of Starbucks, delicious coffee may come to mind, but there's another key to their success – their loyalty program! 🏅

Starbucks introduced a <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Ftiered&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#tiered</a> rewards system through their Starbucks Rewards program, using "Stars" as their point currency. This system is designed to encourage different ways to participate and earn more rewards.

💡This smart loyalty strategy did more than just offer rewards — it created an engaging experience that encouraged customers to return more often and spend more. The result? A 7% increase in sales and stronger customer loyalty.

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Fintech Software Development in Numbers 🔢

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/gartner?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Gartner</a>’s recent insights offer a deep dive into the trends and challenges shaping fintech software development!

Here are the key insights: 
🔸 Security and integration remain key hurdles for finance software buyers.
🔸 72% of finance businesses are increasing their software budgets, with IT security and management as top priorities.
🔸 67% of finance companies require 3-6 months to select new software, with reviews playing a critical role.
🔸 70% of buyers report regret, driven by unexpected costs and excessive complexity.
🔸 31% attempted to renegotiate contracts due to regret, while 28% opted to cancel entirely.

These insights highlight the need for clear, scalable solutions in fintech software development. As finance organizations continue their digital transformation journeys, making informed software choices will be key to achieving sustainable growth. 

Appcent is here to help you navigate this path with tailored, secure, and efficient solutions! 📱
